Dear Mr Tanoue
In accordance with our service agreement with the Research Corporation
of the University of Hawaii we have observed the grading work performed during
site grading and building construction at the project site from August 23 2010 to
August 16 2012 The results of our observations are provided in our report
entitled Earthwork Observation and Compaction Testing Report dated
I certify that Geolabs Inc observed the grading work performed for the
project To the best of our knowledge it is our professional opinion that the grading
work Item No 13 of the Special Inspection form observed by Geolabs was
constructed in general conformance with the plans and specifications and our
geotechnical engineering report prepared for the project

Dear Mr Sumida
This report summarizes our geotechnical engineering observations and testing services
performed during mass and site grading utility installation and foundation preparation for the
University of Hawaii West Oahu Campus Phase 1 project from August 23 2010 to August 16
2012 in accordance with our fee proposal dated August 4 2010
PROJECT CONSIDERATIONS
The University of Hawaii West Oahu Campus covers approximately 103 5 acres and is
south and east of Farrington Highway and west of North South Road in the Ewa District on
the Island of Oahu Hawaii New building structures and supporting infrastructure installation
are planned for the Phase 1 campus development The location of the project site is shown on
the Project Location Map Plate 1 and the new building structures are shown on the Site Plans
Plates 2 1 to 2 22
University of Hawaii West Oahu
Page 2
W O 5822 30
GEOLABS INC
Hawaii California
Five new building structures and a parking area about 380 feet by 700 feet were
constructed for the Phase 1 development One of the planned buildings Administration
Building and a parking area about 200 feet by 480 feet were not constructed
The infrastructure for the development included the installation of new underground
utilities such as water sewer and drain lines In addition an entrance road from Farrington
Highway was constructed Based on the grading plans cuts and fills up to about 8 feet were
planned for the project Deeper fills are required within the Kaloi Gulch area
A settlement monitoring program was implemented for the deep fills placed within Kaloi
Gulch for the future Road B and the Campus Loop Road Road D The results of the
settlement monitoring program are provided in our report entitled Settlement Monitoring
Report University of Hawaii West Oahu Campus Phase Hawaii dated
This report addresses our field observations and compaction testing services for the
mass and site grading and backfill operations for the project site
MASS AND SITE GRADING AND UTILITY INSTALLATION
We observed the mass and site grading and utility installation work for the University of
Hawaii West Oahu Campus Phase 1 from August 23 2010 to August 16 2012 The mass
and site grading and utility installation consisted of clearing and grubbing fills of up to about 8
feet in depth and placement and compaction of fills and backfills to achieve the design
finished grades Delta Construction performed the mass grading and utility installation work
Jayar Construction performed the site grading for the building foundations During the mass
and site grading and backfilling operations samples of the on site and imported materials
utilized as fill and backfill materials were obtained and transported to our laboratory for testing
The maximum dry densities and optimum moisture contents were established in our laboratory
in general accordance with ASTM D 1557 Modified Proctor and the test results are
summarized on Plate 3
The fill and backfill materials were moisture conditioned to above optimum moisture
content and compacted to a minimum of 90 percent of the maximum dry density as
determined in accordance with ASTM D 1557 In the pavement areas the fill and backfill
materials within 2 feet of the finished subgrade were compacted to a minimum of 95 percent
relative compaction
During the site grading and backfilling operations periodic field density tests were
performed in general accordance with ASTM D 6938 Nuclear Gauge Method Results of the
compaction tests performed are summarized on Plates 4 1 through 4 153 of this report These
tests were performed on the prepared ground surfaces and on constructed fills and backfills at
the site Test locations and elevations were estimated by pacing and interpolating from on site
survey stakes These locations and elevations should be considered accurate only to the
degree implied by the methods used Areas assessed as unsatisfactory were reworked until
University of Hawaii West Oahu
Page 3
W O 5822 30
GEOLABS INC
Hawaii California
the specified minimum compaction was obtained and or approved by our field representative
based on visual observation and hand probing
During the heavy rains in December 2010 water ponding occurred within the trenches
for the building footings The water was removed from the trenches and the soft subgrade
material was removed and replaced with compacted fill material
Our services consisted of full time and part time field observation of the contractor s fill
and backfill placement subgrade preparation and compaction procedures during the above
grading operations
Based on the observations of our field representatives and the results of the referenced
tests it is our opinion that the mass and site grading and backfill installation work for the
University of Hawaii West Oahu Campus Phase 1 project observed and tested by Geolabs in
the period covered by this report was performed in conformance with the general intent of the
following references
1
Chapter 14 of the Revised Ordinances of Honolulu 1990 as amended
2
Report by Geolabs Inc entitled Geotechnical Engineering Exploration
University of Hawaii West Oahu Campus Phase Hawaii dated
LIMITATIONS
Geolabs assumes no responsibility for alterations made to slopes or finished grades on
the above project subsequent to our observation and testing period without our knowledge and
written acknowledgment
It should be noted that it is not possible to continuously observe all activities occurring
simultaneously on a construction site therefore some work may have occurred without our
observation However we believe that the level of earthwork observation and testing services
provided is reasonable in reducing the geotechnical risks to the project It should be
recognized that there are variations in the accuracy and statistical repeatability of the tests and
methods used to monitor the earthwork construction and materials Our services were
performed in accordance with generally accepted standards of geotechnical engineering
practice no warranty is expressed or implied Provision of construction monitoring by an
engineer is not insurance nor does it guarantee construction of any type The contractor shall
retain responsibility for the quality of the work for adhering to the plans and specifications and
for repairing defects regardless of when they are found
University of Hawaii West Oahu Page 4
W O 5822 30

We appreciate the opportunity to be of continued service to you on this project If you
have questions or need additional information please contact our office
Respectfully submitted
